# Hyperlink3r
This generates docx files with illegal hyperlinks. My goal was to find a way to mess with the "Office Editing for Docs, Sheets & Slides" extension and maybe find a way to redirect to javascript:// urls or something but that doesnt actually work but feel free to mess with this ig

